msg:Qingdao MGM Hotel truly offers a grand and affordable experience. The spacious rooms are a highlight, with a bed that can easily accommodate 4-5 people, providing ample room for a comfortable stay. The presence of a mini couch adds a touch of luxury and offers a great spot to enjoy the mesmerizing sea view.

The aesthetics of the toilet are impressive, with a huge light mirror and a flexible mini light mirror that can be adjusted to your liking, making it convenient for personal grooming. The inclusion of a bathtub and a separate shower area caters to various preferences.

One of the standout features is the Dyson hair dryer, known for its efficiency in drying hair quickly. This added amenity enhances the overall guest experience.

The automated toilet seat is a thoughtful touch, as it lifts when you enter and automatically flushes when you leave, providing convenience and maintaining hygiene. Qingdao MGM Hotel certainly combines luxury and affordability, making it a delightful choice for a memorable stay.

msg:Firstly, I must mention the facilities of this hotel. As it is newly opened, all the facilities are extremely new, from the beds and bathrooms in the rooms to the decorations and leisure facilities in the public areas. The hotel's interior design is uniquely stylish, exhibiting a more trendy look compared to other international hotels around this area, giving off a sense of fashion and modernity.
Secondly, despite being located a bit far from the seashore, this did not hinder my appreciation of the sea view. From my room, I could enjoy the beauty of the sea and feel the gentle breeze of the ocean, as if I were on a seaside vacation.
Moving on to the breakfast, it was quite extensive, offering a variety of choices. From traditional Chinese breakfast options to Western bread and milk, there's something for everyone. Both Chinese and Western breakfast lovers can find something to satisfy their taste buds here. Moreover, the quality of the breakfast is excellent, with fresh ingredients and delicious flavors, making it a satisfying meal.
Lastly, I must mention the underground parking lot of this hotel. It provides ample parking spaces, making it very convenient for guests who travel by car. The parking lot is also well-equipped, with dedicated security personnel to oversee the vehicles, giving guests peace of mind when leaving their cars here.

posted:Posted June 8, 2024
msg:Make a very objective evaluation:
First of all, I am very grateful to Miss Elly, the housekeeper at the front desk, for contacting me two days before the trip to communicate what type of trip I would like to go. When she learned that we were staying as a couple, she also helped us arrange the room. She was very considerate and gave her a good reviewüëçüèª
The general service of Qingdao MGM is still up to par. The guy who received us at the door was enthusiastic, helped to open the car door, took the initiative to take the luggage, and sent the luggage upstairs. I especially like Rock, who was easy-going and handsome.
Having experienced MGM all over the world, I can only say that the feeling of each place is different. The MGM in Qingdao is really new, and the hardware facilities are really nothing to say, but some details need to be improved.

The following are some of the shortcomings I experienced personally:

Hygiene: In fact, hygiene is relatively good, not as exaggerated as some comments on the Internet say. A lot of dust is actually closely related to light. It may be because the light from the large floor-to-ceiling windows makes the dust particularly obvious, so the floor and walls appear a little dirty. It is recommended to pay attention to the elevator buttons in the elevator area. This material is not wiped frequently, and it is really easy to get fingerprints and water stains, which looks very unhygienic.

Breakfast: The food is up to standard, with everything, similar to St. Regis and Westin. I stayed for two nights. The first day's breakfast was not yet the Dragon Boat Festival, so there were relatively few people. The second day's breakfast was almost over, and I had to queue up, but fortunately it didn't take long, and I found that there were actually many vacancies. If it is just to limit the flow, let the guests queue up outside early in the morning to eat the buffet breakfast. This arrangement is very inappropriate and does not meet the standards of a big hotel.

Toiletries: No cotton swabs.

Compared with Diaoyutai next door, I stayed for one night, and MGM is still a little bit worse, after all, the price is cheap. Overall, it's not bad, the details need to be improved, but the overall stay is still very comfortable and enjoyable, give a good review!
